       var ns=(document.layers);
                var ie=(document.all);
                var w3=(document.getElementById &amp;&amp; !ie);

                function isIE6OrEarlier() { 
                    // Returns the version of Internet Explorer or a -1 (indicating the use of another browser). 
                    var rv = -1; // Return value assumes failure. 
                    if (navigator.appName == 'Microsoft Internet Explorer') { 
                        var ua = navigator.userAgent; 
                        var re = new RegExp("MSIE ([0-9]{1,}[\.0-9]{0,})"); 
                        if (re.exec(ua) != null) rv = parseFloat( RegExp.$1 ); 
                    } 
                    return (rv != -1 &amp;&amp; rv &lt; 7); 
                }

                function getClientWidth() {
                    var clientW = 0;
                    if (top.window.innerWidth) { 
                        clientW = top.window.innerWidth; // ns4
                    } else if(top.document.body) {
                        clientW = top.document.body.clientWidth;
                        if (top.document.body.offsetWidth == clientW &amp;&amp; top.document.documentElement &amp;&amp; top.document.documentElement.clientWidth) {
                            clientW = top.document.documentElement.clientWidth;
                        }
                    }
                    return clientW;
                }

                function getClientHeight() {
                    var clientH = 0;
                    if (window.innerHeight) { 
                        clientH = window.innerHeight; // ns4
                    } else if(document.body) {
                        clientH = document.body.clientHeight;
                        if (document.body.offsetHeight == clientH &amp;&amp; document.documentElement &amp;&amp; document.documentElement.clientHeight) {
                            clientH = document.documentElement.clientHeight;
                        }
                    }
                    return clientH;
                }

                function setClientWidthAndHeight() {
                    if (!isIE6OrEarlier()) {
                        document.write('&lt;div style=\'display:none;\'&gt;&lt;img src=\'/setclientsize.asp?w='+getClientWidth()+'&amp;h='+getClientHeight()+'\' width=\'1\' height=\'1\'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
                    }
                    return true;
                }			  
              if (typeof detimg == "undefined") {
                setClientWidthAndHeight();
			    
			    if(document.cookie) {
			    
				  var detimg = document.createElement("img");
				  detimg.src = '/js.asp?sid=606401439';
				  detimg.width = '1';
				  detimg.height = '1';					
			    
			    }
			    
			  }

            function randomXToY(minVal,maxVal,floatVal) {
              var randVal = minVal+(Math.random()*(maxVal-minVal));
              return typeof floatVal=='undefined'?Math.round(randVal):randVal.toFixed(floatVal);
            }
            
            function findClosest(arr, id, increasing) {
                var step = increasing ? 1 : -1;
                for(var i=id+step; i&gt;=0 &amp;&amp; i&lt;=arr.length; i+=step)
                    if( arr[id] )
                        return id;
            }

			function activeimgbtm(oimg) {						
				if (oimg) {
					oimg.src = oimg.src.replace(/.gif$/, "_hot.gif");
                    oimg.src = oimg.src.replace(/.png$/, "_hot.png");
					return true;
				}
			}

					return true;
				}
			}

			function formvalidator(theform) {
				if (jQuery('#search_loading').exists()) {
					jQuery('#search_loading').css('display','none');	
				}
	            
				if (theform.searchname.value == '' || theform.searchname.value == 'suchen...') {
					theform.searchname.value = '';
					theform.searchname.style.color = '#000';	    
					theform.searchname.select();
	                
					return (false);
				}
	            
				if ((theform.searchname.value.length &lt; 2) || (theform.searchname.value.length &gt; 100)) {
					theform.searchname.select();
					alert("Bitte geben Sie mindestens 2 Zeichen ein!");
					return (false);
				}
				if (jQuery('#search_loading').exists()) {
					jQuery('#search_loading').css('display','inline');	
				}
	            
				return (true);
			}

			function openhelp() {
				window.open("/help/default.asp?l=d&amp;w=p","_blank","width=672,height=550,left=,top=,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,status=no,menubar=no,directories=no,location=no,toolbar=no");
				return false;
			}

			function printdoc() {
				var browserVersion = parseInt(navigator.appVersion)
				if (browserVersion &gt;= 4) {
					if (top.cumain) {
						top.cumain.cucontent.focus();
						top.cumain.cucontent.print();
						return false;
					} else {
						if (self == top) {
							window.print();
							return false;
						} else {
							return true;
						}
					}
				} else {
					return true;
				}
			}

            function SubmitWLForm(thisform) {
          
                if (checkValues(thisform) == true) {
                    
					var sWidth = 475
					var sHeight = 270
					
					var params = jQuery("#wishlistform").serialize();
					var url = sLanguagePrefix+"/community/list_add.asp?" + params;
                  
					LoadPopup(url, sWidth, sHeight, false);
					
                }

                return false;

            };

            reportError = function (request) {
                jQuery('#popup_layer').html("Error");
            };

            function isalphanumeric(sThisValue, wishlist) {
                if (wishlist == true) {
                    var alphanum = /^[0-9A-Z\_\ \-]+$/i;
                }
                else {
                    var alphanum = /^[0-9A-Z\_\ \-\\\\]+$/i;
                }
                if (alphanum.test(sThisValue)) {
                    return true;
                }
                return false;
            }

            var sPrefix = "\n- ";
            var oFocus = "";
            var language = "deutsch";	

            checkValues = function (thisForm) {
          
                //Error Strings
                var sErrorDE = "";
                var sErrorEN = "";
                var sVErrorDE = "";
                var sVErrorEN = "";
                var oFocus = thisForm;

                //Alle Felder auslesen!!!
                var cLists = thisForm.Lists;
                var cNewNote = thisForm.NewNote;
                var cNewWishlist = thisForm.NewWishlist;
                var sNewNoteName = thisForm.NewNoteName.value;
                var sNewWishlistName = thisForm.NewWishlistName.value;
                var iAmount = thisForm.Amount.value;

                //Vorgang
                bChecked = false;
                  
                for (i = 0; i &lt;= cLists.length - 1; i++) {
                    if (cLists[i].checked) {
                        bChecked = true;
                    }
                }

                if (bChecked == false) {
                    sErrorDE += sPrefix + "Wunsch-/Merkzettel auswhlen";
                    sErrorEN += sPrefix + "Select wish list/note";
                }

                if (cNewNote.checked == true) {
                    if (sNewNoteName == "") {
                        sErrorDE += sPrefix + "Bezeichnung fr neuen Merkzettel eingeben";
                        sErrorEN += sPrefix + "Enter title for new note";
                        if (oFocus == thisForm) {
                            oFocus = thisForm.NewNoteName;
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (isalphanumeric(sNewNoteName, false) != true) {
                            sErrorDE += sPrefix + "Keine Sonderzeichen fr den Namen verwenden";
                            sErrorEN += sPrefix + "Don't use special characters for note name";
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (cNewWishlist.checked == true) {
                    if (sNewWishlistName == "") {
                        sErrorDE += sPrefix + "Bezeichnung fr neuen Wunschzettel eingeben";
                        sErrorEN += sPrefix + "Enter Title for new wish list";
                        if (oFocus == thisForm) {
                            oFocus = thisForm.NewWishlistName;
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (isalphanumeric(sNewWishlistName, true) != true) {
                            sErrorDE += sPrefix + "Keine Sonderzeichen fr den Wunschzettel Namen verwenden";
                            sErrorEN += sPrefix + "Don't use special characters for wish list name";
                        }
                    }
                }
               
                if (iAmount == "") {
                    sErrorDE += sPrefix + "Menge eingeben";
                    sErrorEN += sPrefix + "Enter quantity";
                    if (oFocus == thisForm) {
                        oFocus = thisForm.Amount;
                    }
                }

                if (isNaN(iAmount)) {
                    sErrorDE += sPrefix + "Numerische Menge eingeben";
                    sErrorEN += sPrefix + "Enter numeric quantity";
                    if (oFocus == thisForm) {
                        oFocus = thisForm.Amount;
                    }
                }

                //Fehlerausgabe
                
                if (sErrorDE != "" &amp;&amp; language == "deutsch") {
                    sErrorDE = "Folgende Fehler sind aufgetreten:\n" + sErrorDE;
                    alert(sErrorDE);
                    oFocus.focus();
                    return false;
                }
                if (sErrorEN != "" &amp;&amp; language == "english") {
                    sErrorEN = "The following error occured:\n" + sErrorEN;
                    alert(sErrorEN);
                    oFocus.focus();
                    return false;
                }
                
                return true;

            }

            checkNameValues = function (thisForm, isWishlist) {
     
                //Error Strings
                var sErrorDE = "";
                var sErrorEN = "";
                var sVErrorDE = "";
                var sVErrorEN = "";
                var oFocus = thisForm;

                //Alle Felder auslesen!!!
                var sNewListName = thisForm.NewListName.value;
             
                if (isWishlist == false) {
                    if (sNewListName == "") {
                        sErrorDE += sPrefix + "Bezeichnung fr neuen Merkzettel eingeben";
                        sErrorEN += sPrefix + "Enter title for new Note";
                        if (oFocus == thisForm) {
                            oFocus = thisForm.NewListName;
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (isalphanumeric(sNewListName, false) != true) {
                            sErrorDE += sPrefix + "Keine Sonderzeichen fr den Merkzettel Namen verwenden";
                            sErrorEN += sPrefix + "Don't use special characters for Note name";
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (isWishlist == true) {
                    if (sNewListName == "") {
                        sErrorDE += sPrefix + "Bezeichnung fr neuen Wunschzettel eingeben";
                        sErrorEN += sPrefix + "Enter title for new Wish List";
                        if (oFocus == thisForm) {
                            oFocus = thisForm.NewListName;
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (isalphanumeric(sNewListName, true) != true) {
                            sErrorDE += sPrefix + "Keine Sonderzeichen fr den Wunschzettel Namen verwenden";
                            sErrorEN += sPrefix + "Don't use special characters for Wish List name";
                        }
                    }
                }

                //Fehlerausgabe

                if (sErrorDE != "" &amp;&amp; language == "deutsch") {
                    sErrorDE = "Folgende Fehler sind aufgetreten:\n" + sErrorDE;
                    alert(sErrorDE);
                    oFocus.focus();
                    return false;
                }
                if (sErrorEN != "" &amp;&amp; language == "english") {
                    sErrorEN = "The following error occured:\n" + sErrorEN;
                    alert(sErrorEN);
                    oFocus.focus();
                    return false;
                }

                return true;

            }

            function checkSearchValues(thisForm)
            {
                var sError = "";
                var oFocus = thisForm;
               
	            var sFirstname = thisForm.firstname.value;
                var sLastname = thisForm.lastname.value;
                var sCity = thisForm.city.value;
                var sEmail = thisForm.email.value;
	 
	            if((sFirstname == "" || sLastname == "" || sCity == "") &amp;&amp; sEmail == "")
	            {
	                if (language != "english")
	                {
	                sError = "Bitte geben Sie den vollstndigen Name und den Wohnort ein, oder suchen Sie nach einer E-Mail-Adresse!";
                    }
                    else
                    {
                    sError = "Please enter full name and city or search by e-mail address!";
                    }
                    alert(sError);
                    oFocus.focus();
	                return false;
	            }
                return true;
            }

		            return true;
	            }
            }

	            if (oimg) {
		            oimg.src = oimg.src.replace(/_hot.png$/, ".png");
		            return true;
	            }
